time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_R26-d3_1.fastq --aligned R26-d3_aligned --other R26-d3_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv R26-d3_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_R26-d3_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_R26-d3_1.fastq;

mv sort_R22-CR-d5_1_screen* qa/fastq_screen;

time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_R22-CR-LC-d5_1.fastq --aligned R22-CR-LC-d5_aligned --other R22-CR-LC-d5_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv R22-CR-LC-d5_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_R22-CR-LC-d5_1.fastq;

time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_R24-LC-d5_1.fastq --aligned R24-LC-d5_aligned --other R24-LC-d5_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv R24-LC-d5_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_R24-LC-d5_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_R24-LC-d5_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 R24-LC-d5_aligned.fastq;
mv R24-LC-d5_aligned.fastq.gz sortmerna/;
mv R24-LC-d5_aligned.log log/;
fastqc -o qa/sortmerna sortmerna/sort_R24-LC-d5_1.fastq;
mkdir STAR/R24-LC-d5;
~/STAR-2.7.0f/bin/Linux_x86_64/STAR --genomeDir /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/ --readFilesIn sortmerna/sort_R24-LC-d5_1.fastq --runThreadN 10 --outFileNamePrefix STAR/R24-LC-d5/R24-LC-d5 --outFilterMultimapNmax 1 --outSAMtype BAM SortedByCoordinate;
pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_R24-LC-d5_1.fastq;
cp STAR/R24-LC-d5/R24-LC-d5Log.final.out log/R24-LC-d5_STAR.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes STAR/R24-LC-d5/R24-LC-d5Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count/R24-LC-d5_union_name.count;

mv sort_R24-LC-d5_1_screen* qa/fastq_screen;

time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_R24-CR-d7_1.fastq --aligned R24-CR-d7_aligned --other R24-CR-d7_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv R24-CR-d7_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-d7_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_R24-CR-d7_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 R24-CR-d7_aligned.fastq;
mv R24-CR-d7_aligned.fastq.gz sortmerna/;
mv R24-CR-d7_aligned.log log/;
fastqc -o qa/sortmerna sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-d7_1.fastq;
mkdir STAR/R24-CR-d7;
~/STAR-2.7.0f/bin/Linux_x86_64/STAR --genomeDir /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/ --readFilesIn sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-d7_1.fastq --runThreadN 10 --outFileNamePrefix STAR/R24-CR-d7/R24-CR-d7 --outFilterMultimapNmax 1 --outSAMtype BAM SortedByCoordinate;
pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-d7_1.fastq;
cp STAR/R24-CR-d7/R24-CR-d7Log.final.out log/R24-CR-d7_STAR.log;

time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_R24-CR-LC-d9_1.fastq --aligned R24-CR-LC-d9_aligned --other R24-CR-LC-d9_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv R24-CR-LC-d9_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-LC-d9_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_R24-CR-LC-d9_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 R24-CR-LC-d9_aligned.fastq;
mv R24-CR-LC-d9_aligned.fastq.gz sortmerna/;
mv R24-CR-LC-d9_aligned.log log/;
fastqc -o qa/sortmerna sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-LC-d9_1.fastq;
mkdir STAR/R24-CR-LC-d9;
~/STAR-2.7.0f/bin/Linux_x86_64/STAR --genomeDir /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/ --readFilesIn sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-LC-d9_1.fastq --runThreadN 10 --outFileNamePrefix STAR/R24-CR-LC-d9/R24-CR-LC-d9 --outFilterMultimapNmax 1 --outSAMtype BAM SortedByCoordinate;
pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-LC-d9_1.fastq;
cp STAR/R24-CR-LC-d9/R24-CR-LC-d9Log.final.out log/R24-CR-LC-d9_STAR.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes STAR/R24-CR-LC-d9/R24-CR-LC-d9Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count/R24-CR-LC-d9_union_name.count;
~/fastq_screen_v0.11.1/fastq_screen --aligner bwa --threads 10 --conf /mnt/f/Genomes/fastq_screen/fastq_screen.conf sortmerna/sort_R24-CR-LC-d9_1.fastq.gz;
mv sort_R24-CR-LC-d9_1_screen* qa/fastq_screen;
